9-32 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 14, 2016 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Meghan Wolff and Marc Calderaro











We all know since Pro Tour Eldritch Moon you’re itching for some new decklists. I mean, the Top 8 is good and all, but it’s really only part of the story, now isn’t it?


Don’t worry, we’ve got you covered.
